# MAIN_IMAGE_RED
+ General SCIL statements

++ Basic SCIL statements
"[@]name[component] = value", "Assigns a value to a variable"
"#ARGUMENT name [,name,...,name]", "Declares arguments of the program"
"#BLOCK ... #BLOCK_END", "Compounds statements into one", "#BLOCK", "", "#BLOCK_END"
"#CASE ... #CASE_END", "Multibranched conditional execution", "#CASE expression", "[#WHEN selector statement]", "[#OTHERWISE statement]", "#CASE_END"
"#DO program", "Executes the SCIL program given as an argument"
"#ERROR IGNORE", "Defines the error handling policy: Execution continues, no error handlers are called or no messages are produced"
"#ERROR CONTINUE", "Defines the error handling policy: Error handling program/message is activated, but execution continues"
"#ERROR STOP", "Defines the error handling policy: Error handling program/message is activated, and execution is aborted"
"#ERROR EVENT", "Defines the error handling policy: Error handling program is activated and execution is aborted"
"#ERROR RAISE [status]", "Raises a SCIL error"
"#IF ... #THEN", "Conditional execution", "#IF condition1 #THEN statement1", "#ELSE_IF condition2 #THEN statement2", "#ELSE statement3"
"#LOCAL  name [= value] [,name [= value],,,name [= value]]", "Declares local variables of the program"
"#LOOP ... #LOOP_END", "Executes a sequence of statements in a loop", "#LOOP [condition]", "", "#LOOP_END [max]"
"#LOOP_WITH ... #LOOP_END", "Executes a loop a number of times", "#LOOP_WITH var = low .. high", "", "#LOOP_END"
"#LOOP_EXIT", "Interrupts the innermost loop it is textually located in"
"#ON event [statement]", "Declares a program block to be executed when an event occurs"
"#ON ERROR [statement]", "Defines an error handler"
"#ON KEY_ERROR [statement]", "Defines a key error handler"
"#PAUSE interval", "Takes a pause"
"#RETURN [value]", "Stops the program execution and returns a value to the caller"
"#SET_TIME time", "Sets the system time"

++ Application and system object commands
"#CREATE object [=attributes]", "Creates a new application or base system object"
"#DELETE object", "Deletes an application object or an attribute of a variable object"
"#EXEC object [(variable_list)]", "Queues an application object for execution"
"#EXEC_AFTER delay object [(variable_list)]", "Queues an application object for execution after a time delay"
"#GET object", "Updates process object values"
"#INIT_QUERY n [condition]", "Initiates a process query"
"#MODIFY object = attributes", "Changes an application object definition"
"#SEARCH n apl type order [start [condition]]", "Initializes a search among objects"
"#SET object_attribute [= value]", "Assigns a value to an attribute of a system or application (except event) object"

++ Printout commands
"#LIST printer object [(variable_list)]", "Prints process object data"
"#PRINT printer picture [(variable_list)]", "Prints a picture"

++ Path commands
"#PATH name [+|-] [dir, ..., dir]", "Defines a logical path"
"#REP_LIB library [+|-] [file, ..., file]", "Defines a logical representation library"

++ File handling commands
"#CLOSE_FILE n", "Closes a keyed file"
"#CREATE_FILE n apl file keylength", "Creates and opens a new keyed file"
"#DELETE_FILE apl file", "Deletes a file"
"#OPEN_FILE n apl file keylength", "Opens a keyed file"
"#READ n key data1 [data2]", "Reads a data record from a keyed file"
"#READ_KEYS n vector [key1 [key2]]", "Reads the keys of a keyed file"
"#READ_NEXT n key result1 [result2]", "Reads a data record next to ''key'' from a keyed file"
"#READ_PREV n key result1 [result2]", "Reads a data record previous to ''key'' from a keyed file"
"#REMOVE n key", "Deletes a data record from a keyed file"
"#RENAME_FILE apl old new", "Renames a file"
"#WRITE n data1 [data2]", "Writes a data record into a keyed file"

+ Visual SCIL commands

++ Loading, creating and deleting Visual SCIL objects
".CREATE object = type [(attribute = value, ..., attribute = value)]", "Creates a Visual SCIL object"
".DELETE object", "Deletes a Visual SCIL object"
".LOAD object = type(file, name [, attr = value, attr = value, ...])", "Loads a Visual SCIL object"

++ Handling Visual SCIL attributes
"[object].method [(argument,,,,argument)]", "Calls a method"
".MODIFY object = list", "Modifies one or more attributes of a Visual SCIL object"
".SET [object].attribute[component,,,component] = value", "Assigns a value to a user interface attribute"


+ VS objects, windows and picture functions

++ Methods
"_FLAG_FOR_EXECUTION(name, program [, delay])", "Indicates that the object should execute a SCIL program in the future"
"_QUEUE_FOR_EXECUTION(program [, delay])", "Used when the programmer wants to execute a SCIL program at a later point in time when the system is idle"

++ Attributes
"_COMPILED", "When the attribute is set to TRUE, the all Visual SCIL object and all its child objects that are loaded together are recursively flagged to be compiled"
"_FILE_REVISION", "Contains the FILE_REVISION attribute of the picture file where the window was loaded from"
"_ATTRIBUTE_NAMES", "List of the user-defined attribute names and the names of the attributes defined by the object class"
"_CHILD_OBJECTS", "The names of the immediate children of the object listed in the order of creation"
"_OBJECT_CLASS", "The name of the class of the object"
"_OBJECT_NAME", "The name of the object"
"_OBJECT_PATH", "ROOT-relative object path of the object or the window (including the leading ROOT\)"
"_SOURCE_FILE_NAME", "The full operating system format name of the VSO or PIC file where the object has been loaded or read from"
"_VARIABLE_NAMES", "The names of SCIL variables defined in the SCIL context that the object belongs to"
"_SG_GEOMETRY", "The geometry of a window or a picture function"

+ Picture handling commands

++ General picture handling commands
"!CLOSE", "Closes the monitor"
"!FAST_PIC [-] [picture], [-] [picture], ...", "Adds and removes fast picture definitions in semi-graphic monitors"
"!INT_PIC", "Displays an alarm picture"
"!LAST_PIC", "Displays the previous picture"
"!NEW_PIC picture", "Displays a picture"
"!RECALL_PIC", "Recalls a stored picture name"
"!RESTORE", "Stops function key blinking"
"!STORE_PIC", "Stores the present picture name"
"!UPDATE interval", "Defines the update time interval"

++ Window handling commands
"!ERASE [picture_path]window", "Erases a window from the screen"
"!SHOW [picture_path]window [expression]", "Shows a window"
"!SHOW_BACK [picture_path]window [expression]", "Shows the picture background of a window"
"!WIN_BG_COLOR [picture_path]window color", "Specifies the color of the background behind the window"
"!WIN_CREATE [picture_path]window", "Creates a window"
"!WIN_INPUT [picture_path]window expression", "Assigns a window an expression"
"!WIN_LEVEL [picture_path]window level", "Specifies the level parameter of the window"
"!WIN_NAME [picture_path]window", "Creates a new window"
"!WIN_PIC [picture_path]window picture", "Selects a picture to be shown in the window"
"!WIN_POS [picture_path]window pos", "Positions a window"
"!WIN_REP [picture_path]window representation", "Selects a library representation for a window"

++ Input commands
"!CSR_LEFT", "Move the data entry cursor one step to the left"
"!CSR_RIGHT", "Move the data entry cursor one step to the right"
"!CSR_BOL", "Moves the data entry cursor to the beginning of the input field"
"!CSR_EOL", "Moves the data entry cursor to the end of the input field"
"!ENTER", "Completes data entry"
"!INPUT_KEY keytext var", "Reads function key information"
"!INPUT_POS var", "Reads mouse or cursor position"
"!INPUT_VAR [picture path]window variable max_length", "Reads an input value from the user"
"!RUBOUT", "Deletes the character to the left of the input cursor"
"!RUBOUT_CUR", "Deletes the character in the current position of the cursor"
"!RUBOUT_BOL", "Deletes the beginning of the line until, but not including, the cursor"
"!RUBOUT_EOL", "Deletes the end of line starting from the cursor position"
"!TOGGLE_MOD", "Shifts from type-over (default) to insert and vice versa"

++ Miscellaneous picture commands
"!SEND_PIC device number", "Copies the picture (semi-graphic) to a printer"
"!RESET", "Deletes variables in a picture"

+ Primitive graphics commands

++ Full graphics SCIL commands
".ARC [[scope,] n :] x, y, r, a1, a2 [, FILL]", "Draws one or several arcs as circle segment arcs"
".BOX [[scope,] n :] x, y, width, height [, FILL]", "Draws one or several boxes (rectangles)"
".CIRCLE [[scope,] n :] x, y, r [, FILL]", "Draws one or several circles"
".ELLIPSE [[scope,] n :] x, y, a, b [, FILL]", "Draws one or more ellipses"
".IMAGE [[scope,] n :] x, y, w, h, filename [,[tag_8_10]] [,[tag_12_15]] [,[tag_16_20]] [,tag_20_25]", "Draws a VS_IMAGE object into the current window or VS object"
".LINE [[scope,] n :] x1, y1, x2, y2", "Draws one or more lines from (x1, y1) to (x2, y2)"
".POINT [[scope,] n :] x, y, [, RELATIVE]", "Draws one or several points of one pixel''s size at the coordinates (x,y)"
".POLYLINE [[scope,] n :] x, y [, RELATIVE] [, FILL]", "Draws a polyline or a polygon"
".TEXT [[scope,] n :] x, y, text [, FILL] [, EXTENDED] [, align]", "This command draws horizontal text starting at (x, y)"

++ Graphics contexts
".GC [[scope,] n [=[scope,] m]]:[[component = value]...[, component = value]]", "Modifies the graphics context number ''n''"
".COLOR [scope,] number : color [, SHARED|PRIVATE]", "Defines the color mix number"
"COLOR([scope,] number)", "Returns the RGB values of the color"
".FONT [scope,] number:font", "Defines a font number"
"FONT([scope,] number)", "Returns the attributes of the font"
"GC([scope,] n)", "Returns the values of the components of the context"
"COLOR_IN([scope,] n)", "Returns the RGB values of the foreground color in the context"
"FONT_IN([scope,] n)", "Returns the attributes of the font"

++ Graphics canvas
".CANVAS object", "Selects the named picture or dialog object"
".CANVAS ROOT|PARENT|CURRENT", "The root, parent or current object is used as canvas"
".COORDINATE_SYSTEM coordinate_system", "Specifies the coordinate system to be used"
".SCALING [s]", "Sets the scaling factor to be used in the subsequent SCIL graphics commands"
".MOUSE x, y [, button [, buttons [, RELATIVE]]]", "Reads the SCIL coordinates of the cursor and the mouse button states"
".MOUSE ON [, MOTION]", "Sets the program in tracing state"
".MOUSE DISCARD", "Reads and discards all the pending mouse clicks"
".MOUSE OFF", "Ends the tracing state"

++ Miscellaneous graphical commands
".PUSH", "Stores the current canvas selection, scaling factor and graphics contexts definitions"
".POP", "Restores the selections stored with .PUSH"
".FLUSH", "Forces a blink timing and an immediate updating of the entire application window"
".PEND ON", "The graphics drawing is not shown on screen"
".PEND OFF", "The graphics drawing on screen is enabled"


+ Functions

++ Generic functions
"CASE(selector, w1, v1 [, wi, vi]* [, ""OTHERWISE"", vo])", "Selects one of the arguments according to the selector argument value"
"CHOOSE(v)", "Chooses the first non-empty argument"
"CHOOSE(v1, v2, [vi]*)", "Chooses the first non-empty argument"
"DATA_TYPE(expression)", "Returns the data type of the argument"
"DUMP(data [,line_length[, ""LOCALIZED""]])", "Creates a text vector that represents the contents of any SCIL data in SCIL expression syntax"
"ELEMENT_LENGTH(vl)", "The lengths of vector elements and list attributes"
"EQUAL(v1, v2, [,status_handling [,case_policy]]))", "Compares two SCIL values for equality"
"EVALUATE(expression)", "Evaluates an expression given as text in SCIL syntax"
"GET_STATUS(data)", "Returns the status code(s) of a value"
"IF(condition, truevalue, falsevalue)", "Selects one of two arguments according to a given condition"
"LENGTH(arg)", "Returns the length of the argument"
"SET_STATUS(source, status)", "Modifies the status code of SCIL data"
"TYPE_CAST(source, type)", "Views data as if it were of different data type"

++ Arithmetic functions
"ABS(arg)", "The absolute value"
"ARCCOS(arg)", "Arcus cosinus"
"ARCSIN(arg)", "Arcus sinus"
"ARCTAN(arg)", "Arcus tangens"
"COS(arg)", "The cosine of the argument"
"EVEN(arg)", "Tells whether the argument is even"
"EXP(arg)", "The exponential function. The result is the number e, Neper''s number, raised to the power of the argument"
"HIGH_PRECISION_ADD(n1 [, ..., n32])", "Adds up two or more (up to 31) high precision numbers"
"HIGH_PRECISION_DIV(n1, n2)", "Divides a high precision number by another"
"HIGH_PRECISION_MUL(n1, n2)", "Multiplies two high precision numbers"
"HIGH_PRECISION_SHOW(n [,decimals])", "Displays a high precision number in various formats"
"HIGH_PRECISION_SUB(n1, n2)", "Subtracts a high precision number from another"
"HIGH_PRECISION_SUM(v)", "Calculates the sum of the high precision number elements of a vector"
"LN(arg)", "The natural logarithm"
"MIN(arg1 [, ..., arg32])", "Returns the smallest value in the argument list"
"MAX(arg1 [, ..., arg32])", "Returns the largest value in the argument list"
"ODD(arg)", "Tells whether the argument is odd"
"RANDOM(n1, n2)", "Generates a random number in a given range"
"ROUND(arg [,decimals])", "Rounds off a real value"
"SET_RANDOM_SEED(seed)", "Sets the seed number of the random number generator"
"SIN(arg)", "The sine of the argument"
"SQRT(arg)", "The square root of the argument"
"TRUNC(arg [,decimals])", "Truncates a real value"

++ Time functions
"CLOCK", "The present SYS time with one-second resolution"
"DATE[(time)]", "The date (year, month and day) as text"
"DATE[""FULL""]", "The present full date (year, month and day) as text"
"DATE[(time, ""FULL"")]", "The full date (4-digit year, month and day) as text"
"DAY[(time)]", "The day of month"
"DOW[(time)]", "The day of week. The number of the day counting from Monday, which is number one"
"DOY [(time)]", "The day of year. The number of the day since the beginning of the year"
"HOD[(time)]", "Hours of day. Hours passed since the beginning of the day"
"HOUR[(time)]", "The hour"
"HOY[(time)]", "Hours of year. Hours passed since the beginning of the year"
"HR_CLOCK", "SYS time in seconds and microseconds"
"LOCAL_TIME", "The present local time"
"LOCAL_TIME_ADD(time, s [,ms])", "Adds seconds and milliseconds to given local time"
"LOCAL_TIME_INFORMATION[(time)]", "Returns information on given local time"
"LOCAL_TIME_INTERVAL(from, to)", "The length of the time interval between two local times"
"LOCAL_TO_SYS_TIME(time)", "Converts local time to SYS time"
"LOCAL_TO_UTC_TIME(time)", "Converts local time to UTC time"
"MINUTE[(time)]", "The minute"
"MONTH[(time)]", "The number of the month"
"PACK_TIME(year, month, day, hour, minute, second)", "Creates a SCIL time data value out of its components"
"SECOND[(time)]", "The second"
"SET_CLOCK(time)", "Sets the SYS time"
"SET_LOCAL_TIME(time)", "Sets the local time of the system"
"SET_SYS_TIME(time)", "Sets the SYS time of the system"
"SET_UTC_TIME(time)", "Sets the UTC time of the system"
"SYS_TIME", "The present SYS time"
"SYS_TIME_ADD(time, s [,ms])", "Adds seconds and milliseconds to given SYS time"
"SYS_TIME_INTERVAL(from, to)", "The length of the time interval between two SYS times"
"SYS_TO_LOCAL_TIME(time)", "Converts SYS time to local time"
"SYS_TO_UTC_TIME(time)", "Converts SYS time to UTC time"
"TIME[(time)]", "Date and time as text, excluding seconds"
"TIME[(""FULL"")]", "The present full date and time as text, excluding seconds"
"TIME[(time, ""FULL"")]", "Full date and time as text, excluding seconds"
"TIME_SCAN(string [,resolution [,option1 [,option2]]])", "Interprets a date/time text string"
"TIMEMS[(time [,msecs] [,""FULL""])]", "Full date and time as text, including seconds and milliseconds"
"TIME_ZONE_RULES[(rule)]", "Reads and sets the time zone rules of the system."
"TIMES[(time)]", "Date and time as text, including seconds"
"TIMES[(""FULL"")]", "The present full date and time as text, including seconds"
"TIMES[(time, ""FULL"")]", "Full date and time as text, including seconds"
"TOD[(time)]", "Time of day as text, excluding seconds"
"TODMS[(time [,msecs])]", "Time of day as text, including seconds and milliseconds"
"TODS[(time)]", "Time of day as text, including seconds"
"UTC_TIME", "The present UTC time"
"UTC_TIME_ADD(time, s [,ms])", "Adds seconds and milliseconds to given UTC time"
"UTC_TIME_INTERVAL(from, to)", "The length of the time interval between two UTC times"
"UTC_TO_LOCAL_TIME(time)", "Converts UTC time to local time"
"UTC_TO_SYS_TIME(time)", "Converts UTC time to SYS time"
"WEEK[(time)]", "The number of the week within a year"
"YEAR[(time)]", "The year"

++ String functions
"ASCII(n)", "The ASCII character corresponding to the numeric ASCII code"
"ASCII_CODE(c)", "The numeric ASCII code of the character argument"
"BCD_TO_INTEGER(bcd)", "Converts BCD coded numbers to integers"
"BIN(b)", "Represents bit strings and integers as text in binary format"
"BIN_SCAN(string)", "Creates an integer or real value out of its binary text representation"
"BIT_SCAN(string)", "Creates a bit string out of its text representation"
"CAPITALIZE(text)", "Capitalizes a text"
"COLLECT(v, delimiter)", "Collects text fields into a text, where the fields are delimited by the given delimiter character"
"DEC(value [, length [, decimals]])", "Represents integer and real values as text"
"DEC_SCAN(string)", "Creates an integer or real value out of its decimal text representation"
"EDIT(text, key)", "Simple text editing. Removes spaces and tabs out of a text according to a specified rule"
"HEX(n)", "Represents an integer as text in hexadecimal format"
"HEX_SCAN(string)", "Creates an integer or real value out of its hexa-decimal text representation"
"INTEGER_TO_BCD(int [, digits])", "Represents an integer value as a BCD coded bit string"
"JOIN(delimiter [, a]*)", "Joins text fields into a text"
"LOCATE(string1, string2 [, all]))", "Locates a text string in a text"
"LOWER_CASE(text)", "Converts text to lower case"
"OCT(n)", "Represents an integer as text in octal format"
"OCT_SCAN(string)", "Creates an integer or real value out of its octal text representation"
"PACK_STR(source, type [,length [,byte_order]])", "Creates a text, a bit string or a byte string out of its elements"
"PAD([string, ]filler, length)", "Pads a text with a filler string to given length"
"REPLACE(text, string, new_string)", "Replaces text strings by another string"
"SEPARATE(text, delimiter)", "Extracts fields of a text and returns fields as a text vector"
"SUBSTR(string, start [,length])", "Extracts a substring from a text, bit string or byte string value"
"UNPACK_STR(source [,length [,byte_order]])", "Splits a text, a bit string or a byte string to a vector of its elements"
"UPPER_CASE(text)", "Converts text to upper case"

++ Bit functions
"BIT(a, b)", "The bit value of a given bit ''b'' in a bit string or integer ''a''"
"BIT_AND(a1, a2)", "Bitwise logical AND of the integer or bit string arguments"
"BIT_CLEAR(a [, b1, ..., bn])", "Sets given bits to 0"
"BIT_COMPL(a)", "Logical bit complement of the argument. Calculates the bitwise logical NOT of the argument"
"BIT_MASK(n1, ..., n32)", "Bit mask with given bits set to 1. Calculates an integer number by setting the given bits to 1 and all the others to 0"
"BIT_OR(a1, a2)", "Bitwise logical OR of the integer or bit string arguments"
"BIT_SET(a [, b1, ..., bn])", "Sets given bits to 1. Calculates an integer by setting the bits numbered ''b1'',..., ''bn'' in ''a'' to one"
"BIT_STRING(length [, b1 , ..., bn])", "Creates a bit string by setting given bits to 1 and the other ones to 0"
"BIT_XOR(a1, a2)", "Bitwise logical XOR (exclusive OR) of the integer or bit string arguments"

++ Vector handling functions
"APPEND(v1, v2)", "Appends data to a vector"
"BINARY_SEARCH(v, value)", "Searches an ordered vector by its element contents"
"CLASSIFY(vector, n, low, high)", "Classifies the elements of a vector into size classes and returns the counts of each class"
"CUMULATE(vector)", "Accumulates the elements of the argument vector. Each element n of the result vector is set to the sum of the n first elements of the argument vector"
"DELETE_ELEMENT(v, index [,index2])", "Deletes individual elements (one, range or set) of a vector"
"FIND_ELEMENT(v, value [,start_index [,case_policy]])", "Searches a vector by its element contents"
"HIGH(vector)", "The largest element in a vector"
"HIGH_INDEX(vector)", "The index of the largest element in a vector"
"INSERT_ELEMENT(vector, pos, contents)", "Inserts new elements into a vector"
"INTERP(vector, x)", "Interpolates a value from a curve"
"INVERSE(vector, n, low, high)", "Inverts a curve"
"LOW(vector)", "The smallest element in a vector"
"LOW_INDEX(vector)", "The index of the smallest element in a vector"
"MEAN(vector)", "The mean value of elements of a vector"
"PICK(vector, indexes)", "Picks up specified elements from a vector"
"REMOVE_DUPLICATES(vector [,status_handling [,case_policy]])", "Removes duplicate elements of a vector"
"REVERSE(vector)", "Reverses the order of elements of a vector"
"SELECT(source, condition [, wildcards])", "Selects the elements of a vector or a list of vectors that fulfil given condition. Returns the indices of the matching elements"
"SORT(data [, start [, length]])", "Sorts a vector of numeric (integer, real or time) or text data into ascending order or alphabetical order (ASCII code order)"
"SPREAD(vector, indexes, new_value)", "Replaces vector elements by new value"
"SUM(vector)", "The sum of all the elements of a vector"
"SUM_NEG(vector)", "The sum of the negative elements of a vector"
"SUM_POS(vector)", "The sum of the positive elements of a vector"
"TREND(vector, n)", "Returns the last (‘newest’) elements of a vector"
"VECTOR[([element1, ..., elementn])]", "Creates a vector out of given elements"

++ List handling functions
"ATTRIBUTE_EXISTS(list, attribute)", "Checks whether a list contains given attribute(s)"

"MERGE_ATTRIBUTES(left, right)", "Merges two lists into one"

++ Functions related to hardware and software information

++ Functions related to program execution

"OPS_CALL(command [, option1 [,option2]])", "Executes an operating system command"

++ Functions related to run-time environment
"AEP_PROGRAMS(apl)", "Lists the running Application Extension Programs of an application"

"MEMORY_POOL_USAGE(pool)", "Monitors the usage of memory pools (""LOCAL"", ""GLOBAL"" or ""PROCESS"")"
"REGISTRY(function, key, value_name)", "Reads the registry maintained by Windows operating system"
"SCIL_HOST", "Returns the type and number of the kernel process that is running this SCIL code"

++ Functions related to programming environment
"COMPILE(vector)", "Runs the SCIL compiler"
"MAX_APPLICATION_NUMBER", "Maximum number of application objects"
"MAX_BIT_STRING_LENGTH", "Maximum number of bits in a bit string type value"
"MAX_BYTE_STRING_LENGTH", "Maximum number of bytes in a byte string type value"

"MAX_INTEGER", "Largest possible integer value"
"MAX_LINK_NUMBER", "Maximum number of link objects"
"MAX_LIST_ATTRIBUTE_COUNT", "Maximum number of attributes in a list"

"MAX_NODE_NUMBER", "Maximum number of node objects"
"MAX_OBJECT_NAME_LENGTH", "Maximum length of application and Visual SCIL object names"
"MAX_PICTURE_NAME_LENGTH", "Maximum length of picture names"
"MAX_PRINTER_NUMBER", "Maximum number of printer objects"
"MAX_PROCESS_OBJECT_INDEX", "Maximum number of process objects in a process object group"

"Start-up Execution SE", "Indicates whether the command procedure is executed during application start-up, when reporting is chasing the real time", ":CSE"
"Time Channel TC", "The name of the time channel that runs the command procedure", ":CTC"

++ Storage attributes

"Memory Only MO", "Determines whether the dynamically changing attributes OS, QT and RT are stored on disk or not", ":CMO"


+ Time channels (T)

++ Basic attributes
"Comment CM", "A freely chosen text", ":TCM"
"In Use IU", "Indicates whether the time channel is in use or not", ":TIU"
"Logical Name LN", "The name of the time channel", ":TLN"

"Modification Time ZT", "The time when the object was created or modified", ":TZT"

++ Scheduling
"Condition CD", "Condition for running the time channel", ":TCD"
"Cycle Policy CP", "Specifies whether the cycle (attribute CY) is synchronised to the calendar clock or not", ":TCP"
"Cycle CY", "Time interval between cyclic runs. The cycling starts at synchronisation times", ":TCY"
"Daylight Switch Policy DP", "Specifies the behaviour of the time channel, when the local time of the system switches from standard time to daylight saving time or vice versa", ":TDP"
"Start-up Execution Policy SP", "Specifies how the time channel is scheduled at application start-up", ":TSP"
"Synchronization Unit SU", "Defines how often periodic synchronization takes place", ":TSU"
"Synchronization Time SY", "The time of first synchronization", ":TSY"

++ Paralell execution
"Parallel Execution PE", "Indicates whether the object is executed by a parallel queue or not", ":TPE"
"Parallel Queue PQ", "The number of the parallel queue", ":TPQ"
"Synchronized Execution SX", "Specifies whether the completion of parallel objects of the time channel is waited for before the next non-parallel object is started", ":TSX"

++ Time tagging
"Qualified Begin Time QB", "Registers the realized start time of the latest scheduled run of the time channel with a resolution of one millisecond", ":TQB"
"Qualified End Time QE", "Registers the realized completion time of the latest scheduled run of the time channel with a resolution of one millisecond", ":TQE"
"Qualified Synchronisation Time QS", "Registers the latest scheduled synchronisation time with a resolution of one millisecond", ":TQS"
"Qualified Registration Time QT", "Registers the latest scheduled run time with a resolution of one millisecond", ":TQS"
"Registered Begin Time RB", "Registers the realized start time of the latest scheduled run of the time channel with a resolution of one second", ":TRB"
"Registered End Time RE", "Registers the realized completion time of the latest scheduled run of the time channel with a resolution of one second", ":TRE"
"Registered Synchronization Time RS", "Registers the latest scheduled synchronisation time with a resolution of one second", ":TRS"
"Registration Time RT", "Registers the latest scheduled run time with a resolution of one second", ":TRT"

- "Notification message list", "Attributes of the notification message list", "; Attributes of the notification message list:", "; --------------------------------------------"
- "; t_Event = The user action ""APPLY"" or ""CLOSE"". APPLY means, that the user has accepted the selected file or directory. CLOSE is sent, when the user wants to close the dialog."
- "; t_Caller_Action = The text (method name) defined by the calling tool, e.g. ""ROOT.File_Open""."
- "; t_Path_Mode = The code for the selected path mode (""APL"", ""SC"", ""PATH"" or ""OS"")."
- "; t_Full_Path = The full path for the selected file or directory, respecting the selected path mode. E.g. ""/apl/tutor/pict/1.pic""."
- "; t_Directory = The path from the full path, e.g. ""/apl/tutor/pict/""."
- "; t_File_Name = The file name from the full path, if applicable. E.g. ""1.pic""."
- "; t_Absolute_Full_Path = The full path for the selected file or directory in the operating system path format. E.g. ""c:\sc\apl\tutor\pict\1.pic""."
- "; t_MicroSCADA_Path = The path without the file name in the MicroSCADA relative path format, if valid path can be extracted. E.g. ""/apl/tutor/pict/""."
- "; t_Application_Path = The path without the file name in the application relative path format, if valid path can be extracted. E.g. ""pict/""."
- "; t_Logical_Path = The path without the file name in the logical path format, if valid path can be extracted. E.g. ""PICT""."
- "; t_Absolute_Path = The path without the file name in the operating system path format, e.g. ""c:\sc\apl\tutor\pict""."
-- "; b_Read_Only = TRUE, if the user has checked the ""Read-only"" check box, otherwise FALSE."
- "Handling application relative paths", "Sample handling of application relative paths", "; APL paths not directly supported by WRITE_TEXT or READ_TEXT", "; APL path has to be converted to a SC path before usage"

-- "@i_Status = write_text(.t_File, vector(""Test""))"

- "      #return (%i_Status == 0)", "   #block_end", "", "   #when ""UPDATE"" #block", "      @i_Status = status", "", "      @v_Program_Lines = mdl_Scil_Editor.Get_Program", "      .set ROOT\txt_Program._text_vector = %v_Program_Lines", ""
